\uff09\n\nPython3\n## \u30e1\u30bd\u30c3\u30c9\u5b9a\u7fa9\ndef create_suffix_for_article_attribute_keynames(current_timestamp):\n    current_timestamp_str = str(current_timestamp).strip()\n    current_timestamp_str.strip(\" \")\n    suffix = current_timestamp_str\n    return suffix\n\n\ndef create_article_attribute_keynames(suffix):\n    date_key_name = \"date__\" + suffix\n    agency_key_name = \"agency__\"  + suffix\n    source_key_name = \"source__\" +  suffix\n    return [date_key_name, agency_key_name, source_key_name]\n\n\n# articles_dict\u30aa\u30d6\u30b8\u30a7\u30af\u30c8\u306b\u5024\u3092\u683c\u7d0d\u3059\u308b\u3068\u3044\u3046\u3001\u526f\u4f5c\u7528\u3092\u4f34\u3046\u30e1\u30bd\u30c3\u30c9\ndef register_new_articles(articles_dict, ariticle_title_list, article_agency_list, article_date_list, article_source_list, date_key_name, agency_key_name, source_key_name):\n    for unique_title in set(title_list):\n        tmp_title_list,  tmp_date_list, tmp_source_list, tmp_agency_list = [], [], [], []\n        for (date, title, source, agency) in zip(date_list, title_list, source_list, agency_list):\n            if title == unique_title:\n                tmp_title_list.append(title)\n                tmp_date_list.append(date)\n                tmp_source_list.append(source)\n                tmp_agency_list.append(agency)\n            else:\n                pass\n        articles_dict[unique_title].update({date_key_name:tmp_date_list, agency_key_name:tmp_agency_list, source_key_name:tmp_source_list})\n\n\ndef register_data_to_database_dict(articles_dict, current_timestamp, title_list, agency_list, date_list, source_list):\n    # \u8f9e\u66f8\u306e\u5404\u5c5e\u6027\u60c5\u5831 \u683c\u7d0d\u30ad\u30fc\u540d\u306e\u63a5\u5c3e\u8f9e\u3092\u751f\u6210\n    ### \u8f9e\u66f8\u306e\u5404\u5c5e\u6027\u60c5\u5831 \u683c\u7d0d\u30ad\u30fc\u540d\u306e\u63a5\u5c3e\u8f9e\u3092\u751f\u6210\u306b\u5fc5\u8981\u3068\u306a\u308b\u3001\u73fe\u5728\u6642\u523b\u3092\u53d6\u5f97\u3057\u3066\u6587\u5b57\u5217\u5909\u63db\u3059\u308b\u51e6\u7406\u306f\u3001\u526f\u4f5c\u7528\u3092\u4f34\u3046\u305f\u3081\u3001\u4ee5\u4e0b\u306e\u30e1\u30bd\u30c3\u30c9\u5916\u3067\u5b9f\u884c\u3057\u3001\u30e1\u30bd\u30c3\u30c9\u306b\u306f\u5f15\u6570\u306b\u6e21\u3059\n    current_timestamp_str = current_timestamp\n\n    # suffix\u751f\u6210\u30e1\u30bd\u30c3\u30c9\u306f\u3001\u5f15\u6570\uff08\u73fe\u5728\u6642\u523b\u6587\u5b57\u5217\uff09\u304c\u540c\u3058\u306a\u3089\u3070\u3001\u8fd4\u308a\u5024\u306esuffix\u3082\u540c\u4e00\u306a\u3001\u526f\u4f5c\u7528\u3092\u4f34\u308f\u306a\u3044\u30e1\u30bd\u30c3\u30c9\u3067\u3042\u308b\n    suffix = create_suffix_for_article_attribute_keynames(current_timestamp_str)\n    date_key_name, agency_key_name , source_key_name = create_article_attribute_keynames(suffix)\n\n    # \u8f9e\u66f8\u767b\u9332\u30e1\u30bd\u30c3\u30c9 \u5b9f\u884c\n    ### \u3053\u306e\u30e1\u30bd\u30c3\u30c9\u306f\u8f9e\u66f8\u30aa\u30d6\u30b8\u30a7\u30af\u30c8\u3078\u306e\u30c7\u30fc\u30bf\u767b\u9332\uff08\u4ee3\u5165\uff09\u3092\u884c\u3046\u306e\u3067\u3001\u305d\u308c\u81ea\u4f53\u3001dict\u30aa\u30d6\u30b8\u30a7\u30af\u30c8\u306e\u72b6\u614b\u3092\u5909\u3048\u308b\u526f\u4f5c\u7528\u3092\u8d77\u3053\u3059\n    register_new_articles(articles_dict, title_list, agency_list, date_list, source_list, date_key_name, agency_key_name, source_key_name)\n\n\ndef register_newdate_execute(articles_dict, title_list, ariticle_title_list, article_agency_list, article_date_list, article_source_list):\n    for unique_title in set(title_list):\n        tmp_title_list,  tmp_date_list, tmp_source_list, tmp_agency_list = \u6642\u9593\u3092\u7f6e\u3044\u3066 \u5f8c\u304b\u3089\u8ffd\u52a0\u3057\u305f\u540c\u4e00\u898b\u51fa\u3057\u8a18\u4e8b\u306e\u5c5e\u6027\u9805\u76ee\uff08\u9805\u76ee\u5185\u5bb9\uff09\u306e\u30c7\u30fc\u30bf\u578b\u304c\u3001list\u578b\u3067\u3001\u305d\u306e\u898b\u51fa\u3057\u306e\u8a18\u4e8b\u3092\u6700\u521d\u306b\u6295\u5165\u3057\u305f\u6642\u306b\uff08\u6295\u5165\u3055\u308c\u305f\uff09\u8a18\u4e8b\u306e\u5c5e\u6027\u5185\u5bb9\u306f\u3001\u30ea\u30c6\u30e9\u30eb\u5024\u306b\u6210\u3063\u3066\u3044\u308b\uff08\u578b\u304c\u7d71\u4e00\u3055\u308c\u3066\u3044\u306a\u3044\u3002\u53d6\u308a\u51fa\u3057\u6642\u306b\u30ed\u30b8\u30c3\u30af\u7d71\u4e00\u3067\u304d\u306a\u3044\uff09\n\n####__def register_new_articles \u3092\u66f8\u304d\u63db\u3048\u308b\u3002__\n\n```{Python3:\u66f8\u304d\u63db\u3048\u5f8c}\ndef register_new_articles(articles_dict, ariticle_title_list, article_agency_list, article_date_list, article_source_list):\n    for unique_title in set(title_list):\n        tmp_title_list,  tmp_date_list, tmp_source_list, tmp_agency_list = [], [], [], []\n        for (date, title, source, agency) in zip(date_list, title_list, source_list, agency_list):\n            if title == unique_title:\n                tmp_title_list.append(title)\n                tmp_date_list.append(date)\n                tmp_source_list.append(source)\n                tmp_agency_list.append(agency)\n            else:\n                pass\n        if not(unique_title in articles_dict.keys()): # \u307e\u3060\u3001\u305d\u306e\u898b\u51fa\u3057\u540d\u306e\u8a18\u4e8b\u304c\u8f9e\u66f8\u306b\u767b\u9332\u3055\u308c\u3066\u3044\u306a\u3044\u5834\u5408\n            articles_dict[unique_title].update({'date':tmp_date_list, 'agency':tmp_agency_list, 'source':tmp_source_list})\n        elif unique_title in articles_dict.keys():  # \u904e\u53bb\u306b\u3059\u3067\u306b\u540c\u4e00\u898b\u51fa\u3057\u540d\u306e\u8a18\u4e8b\u304c\u767b\u9332\u3055\u308c\u3066\u3044\u308b\u5834\u5408\u306e\u51e6\u7406\n                [articles_dict[unique_title]['date'].append(element) for element in tmp_date_list]\n                [articles_dict[unique_title]['agency'].append(element) for element in tmp_agency_list]\n                [articles_dict[unique_title]['source'].append(element) for element in tmp_source_list]\n        else:\n            pass\n\n```\n\n####__\uff08 articles_dict\u30aa\u30d6\u30b8\u30a7\u30af\u30c8\u306b\u5024\u3092\u683c\u7d0d\u3059\u308b\u3068\u3044\u3046\u3001\u670d\u4f5c\u7528\u3092\u4f34\u3046\u30e1\u30bd\u30c3\u30c9\ndef register_new_articles(ariticle_title_list, article_agency_list, article_date_list, article_source_list):\n\tfor unique_title in set(title_list):\n\t\ttmp_title_list,  tmp_date_list, tmp_source_list, tmp_agency_list = [], [], [], []\n\t\tfor (date, title, source, agency) in zip(date_list, title_list, source_list, agency_list):\n\t\t\tif title == unique_title:\n\t\t\t\ttmp_title_list.append(title)\n\t\t\t\ttmp_date_list.append(date)\n\t\t\t\ttmp_source_list.append(source)\n\t\t\t\ttmp_agency_list.append(agency)\n\t\t\telse:\n\t\t\t\tpass\n\t\tarticles_dict[unique_title].update({date_key_name:tmp_date_list, agency_key_name:tmp_agency_list, source_key_name:tmp_source_list})\n\n# \u30e1\u30bd\u30c3\u30c9\u5b9f\u884c\nregister_new_articles(title_list, agency_list, date_list, source_list)\n```\n\n<img
